In addition, the guest room is equipped with advanced audio equipment, mini bar and coffee machine, which meets my pursuit of high-quality life. The breakfast selection is also rich and varied, and Hunan rice noodles are especially delicious. The hotel also has an Internet celebrity swimming pool, a very wide field of view, and special photos.
It is worth mentioning that the hotel is very conveniently located, just a few steps away from famous attractions such as Meixi Lake International Culture and Art Center and Yuelu Mountain, and it is also close to shopping malls for eating, drinking and having fun. The hotel also cooperates with Lanxiu City to receive game coins for free, and the children are very happy.
Of course, there were some minor incidents during the check-in process, but the staff handled them very quickly and with a very good attitude.
In short, Changsha Meixi Lake Jinmao Luxury Collection Hotel is still highly recommended. Next time I come to Changsha, I will definitely choose this hotel again!
